========== D:\Pax Historia LOCAL\client\src\api\gameApi.ts ==========

import { type GameState } from "@shared/types/GameState";

const API =
  "http://localhost:3000";

export async function getGameState()
: Promise<GameState> {

  const response =
    await fetch(
      `${API}/game/state`
    );

  return response.json();
}

export async function nextTurn()
: Promise<GameState> {

  const response =
    await fetch(
      `${API}/game/next-turn`,
      {
        method: "POST"
      }
    );

  return response.json();
}

import { use, Suspense } from 'react';
import { type GameState } from '@shared/types/GameState';

// 1. Р’С‹РЅРѕСЃРёРј С„РµС‚С‡ РІ РѕС‚РґРµР»СЊРЅСѓСЋ С„СѓРЅРєС†РёСЋ, РєРѕС‚РѕСЂР°СЏ РєСЌС€РёСЂСѓРµС‚ РїСЂРѕРјРёСЃ

}

========== D:\Pax Historia LOCAL\client\src\components\ScenarioSelector.tsx ==========

import { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { type ScenarioInfo } from '@shared/types/ScenarioInfo';

interface ScenarioSelectorProps {
  onScenarioSelect: (scenarioId: string, countryId: string) => void;
}

export function ScenarioSelector({ onScenarioSelect }: ScenarioSelectorProps) {
  const [scenarios, setScenarios] = useState<ScenarioInfo[]>([]);
  const [selectedScenario, setSelectedScenario] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const [selectedCountry, setSelectedCountry] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);

  useEffect(() => {
    fetch('http://localhost:3000/scenarios/list')
      .then(res => res.json())
      .then(data => {
        setScenarios(data);
        setLoading(false);
      })
      .catch(err => {
        console.error('Failed to load scenarios:', err);
        setLoading(false);
      });
  }, []);

  const handleStartGame = () => {
    if (selectedScenario && selectedCountry) {
      onScenarioSelect(selectedScenario, selectedCountry);
    }
  };

  if (loading) {
    return <div className="loading">Р—Р°РіСЂСѓР·РєР° СЃС†РµРЅР°СЂРёРµРІ...</div>;
  }

  return (
    <div className="scenario-selector">
      <h1>Pax Historia</h1>
      <h2>Р’С‹Р±РµСЂРёС‚Рµ СЃС†РµРЅР°СЂРёР№</h2>
      
      <div className="scenario-list">
        {scenarios.map(scenario => (
          <div
            key={scenario.id}
            className={`scenario-card ${selectedScenario === scenario.id ? 'selected' : ''}`}
            onClick={() => {
              setSelectedScenario(scenario.id);
              setSelectedCountry(null);
            }}
          >
            <h3>{scenario.name}</h3>
            <p className="scenario-period">{scenario.startDate} вЂ” {scenario.endDate}</p>
            <p className="scenario-era">{scenario.era}</p>
            <p className="scenario-description">{scenario.description}</p>
          </div>
        ))}
      </div>

      {selectedScenario && (
        <div className="country-selection">
          <h2>Р’С‹Р±РµСЂРёС‚Рµ СЃС‚СЂР°РЅСѓ</h2>
          <div className="country-list">
            {scenarios
              .find(s => s.id === selectedScenario)
              ?.featuredCountries.map(countryId => (
                <button
                  key={countryId}
                  className={`country-button ${selectedCountry === countryId ? 'selected' : ''}`}
                  onClick={() => setSelectedCountry(countryId)}
                >
                  {countryId}
                </button>
              ))}
          </div>
        </div>
      )}

      {selectedScenario && selectedCountry && (
        <button
          className="start-game-button"
          onClick={handleStartGame}
        >
          РќР°С‡Р°С‚СЊ РёРіСЂСѓ
        </button>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}

========== D:\Pax Historia LOCAL\client\src\map\CountryColors.ts ==========

import type { Country } from '@shared/types/Country';

/**
 * РЎРѕР·РґР°РµС‚ РєР°СЂС‚Сѓ С†РІРµС‚РѕРІ СЃС‚СЂР°РЅ РёР· РёРіСЂРѕРІС‹С… РґР°РЅРЅС‹С…
 */
export function createCountryColorMap(countries: Country[]): Map<string, string> {
  const colorMap = new Map<string, string>();
  
  countries.forEach(country => {
    colorMap.set(country.id, country.color);
  });

  return colorMap;
}

/**
 * РЎС‚Р°РЅРґР°СЂС‚РЅС‹Рµ С†РІРµС‚Р° РґР»СЏ РЅРµР№С‚СЂР°Р»СЊРЅС‹С… С‚РµСЂСЂРёС‚РѕСЂРёР№
 */
export const NEUTRAL_COLOR = '#808080';
export const SELECTED_COLOR = '#FFD700';
export const HOVER_COLOR = '#FFFFFF';

========== D:\Pax Historia LOCAL\client\src\map\GeoJsonLoader.ts ==========

import type { FeatureCollection, Feature, Polygon, MultiPolygon } from 'geojson';
import type { Region } from '@shared/types/map/Region';
import type { Country } from '@shared/types/Country';

export interface MapRegionProperties {
  id: number;
  name: string;
  ownerCountryId: string | null;
  ownerColor: string;
  ownerName: string;
  population: number;
}

export interface GameMapData {
  featureCollection: FeatureCollection<Polygon | MultiPolygon, MapRegionProperties>;
}

/**
 * Р—Р°РіСЂСѓР¶Р°РµС‚ GeoJSON Рё РѕР±РѕРіР°С‰Р°РµС‚ РµРіРѕ РёРіСЂРѕРІС‹РјРё РґР°РЅРЅС‹РјРё
 */
export async function loadGameMapData(
  geoJsonUrl: string,
  regions: Region[],
  countries: Country[]
): Promise<GameMapData> {
  try {
    // Р—Р°РіСЂСѓР¶Р°РµРј GeoJSON
    const response = await fetch(geoJsonUrl);
    const geoJson: FeatureCollection = await response.json();

    // РЎРѕР·РґР°РµРј РєР°СЂС‚Сѓ СЂРµРіРёРѕРЅРѕРІ РґР»СЏ Р±С‹СЃС‚СЂРѕРіРѕ РїРѕРёСЃРєР°
    const regionMap = new Map<number, Region>();
    regions.forEach(region => {
      regionMap.set(region.id, region);
    });

    // РЎРѕР·РґР°РµРј РєР°СЂС‚Сѓ СЃС‚СЂР°РЅ РґР»СЏ Р±С‹СЃС‚СЂРѕРіРѕ РїРѕРёСЃРєР°
    const countryMap = new Map<string, Country>();
    countries.forEach(country => {
      countryMap.set(country.id, country);
    });

    // РћР±РѕРіР°С‰Р°РµРј GeoJSON features РёРіСЂРѕРІС‹РјРё РґР°РЅРЅС‹РјРё
    const enrichedFeatures = geoJson.features.map(feature => {
      // РџС‹С‚Р°РµРјСЃСЏ РЅР°Р№С‚Рё ID СЂРµРіРёРѕРЅР° РІ properties
      // РџСЂРµРґРїРѕР»Р°РіР°РµРј, С‡С‚Рѕ РІ GeoJSON РµСЃС‚СЊ РїРѕР»Рµ 'id' РёР»Рё 'region_id'
      const regionId = feature.properties?.id || feature.properties?.region_id;
      
      let properties: MapRegionProperties = {
        id: regionId || 0,
        name: feature.properties?.name || 'Unknown',
        ownerCountryId: null,
        ownerColor: '#808080', // РЎРµСЂС‹Р№ РґР»СЏ РЅРµР№С‚СЂР°Р»СЊРЅС‹С… С‚РµСЂСЂРёС‚РѕСЂРёР№
        ownerName: 'Neutral',
        population: 0
      };

      // Р•СЃР»Рё РЅР°С€Р»Рё СЂРµРіРёРѕРЅ, РѕР±РѕРіР°С‰Р°РµРј РґР°РЅРЅС‹РјРё
      if (regionId && regionMap.has(regionId)) {
        const region = regionMap.get(regionId)!;
        const ownerCountry = region.ownerCountryId ? countryMap.get(region.ownerCountryId) : null;

        properties = {
          id: region.id,
          name: region.name,
          ownerCountryId: region.ownerCountryId,
          ownerColor: ownerCountry?.color || '#808080',
          ownerName: ownerCountry?.name || 'Neutral',
          population: region.population
        };
      }

      return {
        ...feature,
        properties
      } as Feature<Polygon | MultiPolygon, MapRegionProperties>;
    });

    return {
      featureCollection: {
        type: 'FeatureCollection',
        features: enrichedFeatures
      }
    };
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('РћС€РёР±РєР° Р·Р°РіСЂСѓР·РєРё РґР°РЅРЅС‹С… РєР°СЂС‚С‹:', error);
    throw error;
  }
}

/**
 * РћР±РЅРѕРІР»СЏРµС‚ РґР°РЅРЅС‹Рµ РєР°СЂС‚С‹ РїСЂРё РёР·РјРµРЅРµРЅРёРё РІР»Р°РґРµР»СЊС†РµРІ СЂРµРіРёРѕРЅРѕРІ
 */
export function updateMapData(
  featureCollection: FeatureCollection<Polygon | MultiPolygon, MapRegionProperties>,
  regions: Region[],
  countries: Country[]
): FeatureCollection<Polygon | MultiPolygon, MapRegionProperties> {
  const regionMap = new Map<number, Region>();
  regions.forEach(region => {
    regionMap.set(region.id, region);
  });

  const countryMap = new Map<string, Country>();
  countries.forEach(country => {
    countryMap.set(country.id, country);
  });

  const updatedFeatures = featureCollection.features.map(feature => {
    const regionId = feature.properties.id;
    const region = regionMap.get(regionId);

    if (region) {
      const ownerCountry = region.ownerCountryId ? countryMap.get(region.ownerCountryId) : null;
      
      return {
        ...feature,
        properties: {
          ...feature.properties,
          ownerCountryId: region.ownerCountryId,
          ownerColor: ownerCountry?.color || '#808080',
          ownerName: ownerCountry?.name || 'Neutral',
          population: region.population
        }
      };
    }

    return feature;
  });

  return {
    type: 'FeatureCollection',
    features: updatedFeatures
  };
}

========== D:\Pax Historia LOCAL\client\src\map\MapView.tsx ==========

import { useEffect, useRef, useState } from 'react';
import maplibregl from 'maplibre-gl';
import 'maplibre-gl/dist/maplibre-gl.css';
import type { Region } from '@shared/types/map/Region';
import type { Country } from '@shared/types/Country';
import { loadGameMapData, updateMapData, type GameMapData } from './GeoJsonLoader';

interface MapViewProps {
  regions: Region[];
  countries: Country[];
  onRegionClick?: (regionId: number) => void;
  selectedRegionId?: number | null;
}

export function MapView({ regions, countries, onRegionClick, selectedRegionId }: MapViewProps) {
  const mapContainer = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);
  const map = useRef<maplibregl.Map | null>(null);
  const [mapData, setMapData] = useState<GameMapData | null>(null);
  const [hoveredRegionId, setHoveredRegionId] = useState<number | null>(null);

  // РРЅРёС†РёР°Р»РёР·Р°С†РёСЏ РєР°СЂС‚С‹
  useEffect(() => {
    if (!mapContainer.current) return;

    // РЎРѕР·РґР°РµРј СЌРєР·РµРјРїР»СЏСЂ РєР°СЂС‚С‹ MapLibre
    map.current = new maplibregl.Map({
      container: mapContainer.current,
      style: {
        version: 8,
        sources: {
          'osm-tiles': {
            type: 'raster',
            tiles: ['https://tile.openstreetmap.org/{z}/{x}/{y}.png'],
            tileSize: 256,
            attribution: 'В© OpenStreetMap contributors'
          }
        },
        layers: [
          {
            id: 'osm-tiles',
            type: 'raster',
            source: 'osm-tiles',
            minzoom: 0,
            maxzoom: 19
          }
        ]
      },
      center: [37.6173, 55.7558], // РњРѕСЃРєРІР°
      zoom: 3,
      maxZoom: 10,
      minZoom: 2
    });

    // Р”РѕР±Р°РІР»СЏРµРј РєРѕРЅС‚СЂРѕР»С‹ РЅР°РІРёРіР°С†РёРё
    map.current.addControl(new maplibregl.NavigationControl(), 'top-right');

    return () => {
      map.current?.remove();
    };
  }, []);

  // Р—Р°РіСЂСѓР·РєР° РґР°РЅРЅС‹С… РєР°СЂС‚С‹
  useEffect(() => {
    if (!map.current || regions.length === 0 || countries.length === 0) return;

    const loadMap = async () => {
      try {
        // Р—Р°РіСЂСѓР¶Р°РµРј GeoJSON РёР· public РїР°РїРєРё
        const data = await loadGameMapData('/world-adm1.geojson', regions, countries);
        setMapData(data);

        // Р”РѕР±Р°РІР»СЏРµРј РёСЃС‚РѕС‡РЅРёРє РґР°РЅРЅС‹С…
        if (map.current!.getSource('regions')) {
          (map.current!.getSource('regions') as maplibregl.GeoJSONSource).setData(data.featureCollection);
        } else {
          map.current!.addSource('regions', {
            type: 'geojson',
            data: data.featureCollection
          });

          // Р”РѕР±Р°РІР»СЏРµРј СЃР»РѕР№ РґР»СЏ Р·Р°Р»РёРІРєРё СЂРµРіРёРѕРЅРѕРІ
          map.current!.addLayer({
            id: 'regions-fill',
            type: 'fill',
            source: 'regions',
            paint: {
              'fill-color': ['get', 'ownerColor'],
              'fill-opacity': [
                'case',
                ['boolean', ['feature-state', 'hover'], false],
                0.8,
                0.6
              ]
            }
          });

          // Р”РѕР±Р°РІР»СЏРµРј СЃР»РѕР№ РґР»СЏ РіСЂР°РЅРёС†
          map.current!.addLayer({
            id: 'regions-outline',
            type: 'line',
            source: 'regions',
            paint: {
              'line-color': [
                'case',
                ['boolean', ['feature-state', 'hover'], false],
                '#FFFFFF',
                '#000000'
              ],
              'line-width': [
                'case',
                ['boolean', ['feature-state', 'hover'], false],
                2,
                1
              ]
            }
          });

          // Р”РѕР±Р°РІР»СЏРµРј РѕР±СЂР°Р±РѕС‚С‡РёРєРё СЃРѕР±С‹С‚РёР№
          setupMapInteractions();
        }
      } catch (error) {
        console.error('РћС€РёР±РєР° Р·Р°РіСЂСѓР·РєРё РєР°СЂС‚С‹:', error);
      }
    };

    loadMap();
  }, [regions, countries]);

  // РћР±РЅРѕРІР»РµРЅРёРµ РґР°РЅРЅС‹С… РїСЂРё РёР·РјРµРЅРµРЅРёРё РІР»Р°РґРµР»СЊС†РµРІ
  useEffect(() => {
    if (!map.current || !mapData) return;

    const updatedData = updateMapData(mapData.featureCollection, regions, countries);
    setMapData({ featureCollection: updatedData });

    const source = map.current.getSource('regions') as maplibregl.GeoJSONSource;
    if (source) {
      source.setData(updatedData);
    }
  }, [regions, countries, mapData]);

  // РћР±СЂР°Р±РѕС‚РєР° РІС‹РґРµР»РµРЅРёСЏ СЂРµРіРёРѕРЅР°
  useEffect(() => {
    if (!map.current) return;

    // РЎР±СЂР°СЃС‹РІР°РµРј РїСЂРµРґС‹РґСѓС‰РµРµ РІС‹РґРµР»РµРЅРёРµ
    if (selectedRegionId === null) {
      map.current.setFeatureState({ source: 'regions', id: null }, { selected: false });
      return;
    }

    // Р’С‹РґРµР»СЏРµРј РЅРѕРІС‹Р№ СЂРµРіРёРѕРЅ
    map.current.setFeatureState({ source: 'regions', id: selectedRegionId }, { selected: true });
  }, [selectedRegionId]);

  // РќР°СЃС‚СЂРѕР№РєР° РёРЅС‚РµСЂР°РєС‚РёРІРЅРѕСЃС‚Рё РєР°СЂС‚С‹
  const setupMapInteractions = () => {
    if (!map.current) return;

    // РћР±СЂР°Р±РѕС‚С‡РёРє РЅР°РІРµРґРµРЅРёСЏ РјС‹С€Рё
    map.current.on('mousemove', 'regions-fill', (e) => {
      if (!map.current) return;

      map.current.getCanvas().style.cursor = 'pointer';

      if (e.features && e.features.length > 0) {
        if (hoveredRegionId !== null) {
          map.current.setFeatureState(
            { source: 'regions', id: hoveredRegionId },
            { hover: false }
          );
        }

        const feature = e.features[0];
        hoveredRegionId = feature.id as number;
        setHoveredRegionId(hoveredRegionId);

        map.current.setFeatureState(
          { source: 'regions', id: hoveredRegionId },
          { hover: true }
        );
      }
    });

    // РћР±СЂР°Р±РѕС‚С‡РёРє СѓС…РѕРґР° РјС‹С€Рё
    map.current.on('mouseleave', 'regions-fill', () => {
      if (!map.current) return;

      map.current.getCanvas().style.cursor = '';

      if (hoveredRegionId !== null) {
        map.current.setFeatureState(
          { source: 'regions', id: hoveredRegionId },
          { hover: false }
        );
      }

      setHoveredRegionId(null);
    });

    // РћР±СЂР°Р±РѕС‚С‡РёРє РєР»РёРєР°
    map.current.on('click', 'regions-fill', (e) => {
      if (!map.current || !onRegionClick) return;

      if (e.features && e.features.length > 0) {
        const feature = e.features[0];
        const regionId = feature.properties?.id;

        if (regionId) {
          onRegionClick(regionId);
        }
      }
    });
  };

  return <div ref={mapContainer} style={{ width: '100%', height: '100vh' }} />;
}

  max-width: 1200px;
  margin: 0 auto;
  padding: 2rem;

========== D:\Pax Historia LOCAL\client\src\App.tsx ==========

import { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { type GameState } from '@shared/types/GameState'; // РЈС‚РѕС‡РЅРёС‚Рµ РїСѓС‚СЊ Рє РІР°С€РµРјСѓ С‚РёРїСѓ

export function GameView() {
  // 1. РРЅРёС†РёР°Р»РёР·РёСЂСѓРµРј loading РєР°Рє true СЃСЂР°Р·Сѓ. 
  // Р­С‚Рѕ СѓР±РёСЂР°РµС‚ РЅРµРѕР±С…РѕРґРёРјРѕСЃС‚СЊ РІС‹Р·С‹РІР°С‚СЊ setLoading(true) РІРЅСѓС‚СЂРё useEffect.
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
  const [game, setGame] = useState<GameState | null>(null);
  const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    let ignore = false;

    fetch('http://localhost:3000/game/state')
      .then((response) => {
        if (!response.ok) {
          throw new Error(`HTTP error! status: ${response.status}`);
        }
        // 2. РЇРІРЅРѕ С‚РёРїРёР·РёСЂСѓРµРј РѕС‚РІРµС‚ РѕС‚ СЃРµСЂРІРµСЂР°, С‡С‚РѕР±С‹ РёР·Р±Р°РІРёС‚СЊСЃСЏ РѕС‚ `any`
        return response.json() as Promise<GameState>;
      })
      .then((data) => {
        if (!ignore) {
          setGame(data);
          setLoading(false);
        }
      })
      .catch((err) => {
        if (!ignore) {
          console.error('Fetch error:', err);
          setError(err.message);
          setLoading(false);
        }
      });

    // Cleanup С„СѓРЅРєС†РёСЏ РґР»СЏ РїСЂРµРґРѕС‚РІСЂР°С‰РµРЅРёСЏ СѓС‚РµС‡РµРє РїР°РјСЏС‚Рё Рё race conditions
    return () => {
      ignore = true;
    };
  }, []); // РџСѓСЃС‚РѕР№ РјР°СЃСЃРёРІ = СЌС„С„РµРєС‚ СЃСЂР°Р±Р°С‚С‹РІР°РµС‚ С‚РѕР»СЊРєРѕ РїСЂРё РјР°СѓРЅС‚Рµ

  if (loading) {
    return <div className="flex items-center justify-center h-screen">Р—Р°РіСЂСѓР·РєР° РјРёСЂР°...</div>;
  }

  if (error) {
    return <div className="flex items-center justify-center h-screen text-red-500">РћС€РёР±РєР°: {error}</div>;
  }

  if (!game) {
    return <div className="flex items-center justify-center h-screen">Р”Р°РЅРЅС‹Рµ РЅРµ РЅР°Р№РґРµРЅС‹</div>;
  }

  return (
    <div className="h-screen flex flex-col">
      {/* Р—РґРµСЃСЊ РІР°С€Р° РєР°СЂС‚Р° MapLibre Рё UI */}
      <div className="flex-1 relative">
        {/* <MapView game={game} /> */}
      </div>
      
      <div className="p-4 bg-slate-800 text-white">
        <p>РўРµРєСѓС‰Р°СЏ РґР°С‚Р°: {game.currentDate}</p>
        <p>РРіСЂРѕРє: {game.playerCountryId}</p>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

========== D:\Pax Historia LOCAL\server\src\ai\CountryAction.ts ==========

export interface CountryAction {

  countryId: string;

  category:
    | "economy"
    | "military"
    | "research"
    | "diplomacy"
    | "politics";

  description: string;
}

========== D:\Pax Historia LOCAL\server\src\ai\GenerateCountryActions.ts ==========

import { type Country } from "@shared/types/Country";
import { type CountryAction } from "./CountryAction";

export function generateCountryActions(
  country: Country
): CountryAction[] {

  const actions: CountryAction[] = [];

  if (
    country.goals.length > 0
  ) {

    const goal =
      country.goals[0];

    actions.push({

      countryId: country.id,

      category: "politics",

      description: `РЎС‚СЂРµРјРёС‚СЊСЃСЏ Рє РґРѕСЃС‚РёР¶РµРЅРёСЋ С†РµР»Рё: ${goal.title}`
    });
  }

  return actions;
}

========== D:\Pax Historia LOCAL\server\src\ai\GenerateWorldActions.ts ==========

import { type GameState } from "@shared/types/GameState";
import { type CountryAction } from "./CountryAction";
import { generateCountryActions } from "./GenerateCountryActions";

export function generateWorldActions(
  game: GameState
): CountryAction[] {

  const result: CountryAction[] = [];

  for (
    const country
    of game.countries
  ) {

    result.push(

      ...generateCountryActions(
        country
      )
    );
  }

  return result;
}

import { createCountry } from "./templates/CreateCountry";
import { EconomyType } from "@shared/types/EconomyType";
import { UnitType } from "@shared/types/military/UnitType";

export const USA = createCountry({

  id: "USA",

  name: "United States",

  shortName: "USA",

  color: "#2563eb",

  capitalRegionId: 2,

========== D:\Pax Historia LOCAL\server\src\economy\ProcessEconomy.ts ==========

import { type Country } from "@shared/types/Country";

export function processEconomy(
  country: Country
): void {

  const income =

    country.economy.taxRevenue +

    country.economy.exportIncome +

    country.economy.stateEnterpriseIncome +

    country.economy.otherIncome;

  const expenses =

    country.economy.militarySpending +

    country.economy.researchSpending +

    country.economy.educationSpending +

    country.economy.infrastructureSpending +

    country.economy.welfareSpending +

    country.economy.debtInterest +

    country.economy.otherExpenses;

  const result =
    income - expenses;

  country.economy.treasury += result;

  country.economy.budgetBalance =
    result;
}

========== D:\Pax Historia LOCAL\server\src\events\ApplyEvents.ts ==========

import { type GameState } from "@shared/types/GameState";
import { type SimulationEvent } from "../llm/SimulationResponse";

export function applyEvents(
  game: GameState,
  events: SimulationEvent[]
): void {

  for (const event of events) {

    game.eventHistory.push({

      id: crypto.randomUUID(),

      date: game.currentDate,

      title: event.title,

      description: event.description,

      countries: []
    });
  }
}

========== D:\Pax Historia LOCAL\server\src\game\CreateGame.ts ==========

import { ScenarioRegistry } from "../scenarios/ScenarioRegistry";
import { type GameState } from "@shared/types/GameState";

export function createGame(
  scenarioId: keyof typeof ScenarioRegistry,
  playerCountryId: string
): GameState {
  const scenario = ScenarioRegistry[scenarioId];
  return {
    currentDate: scenario.startDate,
    playerCountryId,
    era: structuredClone(scenario.technologyEra),
    countries: structuredClone(scenario.countries),
    regions: structuredClone(scenario.regions),
    playerActions: [],
    eventHistory: []
  };
}

========== D:\Pax Historia LOCAL\server\src\research\ProcessResearch.ts ==========

import { type Country } from "@shared/types/Country";

export function processResearch(
  country: Country
): void {

  for (
    const project
    of country.technology.projects
  ) {

    project.progress +=
      country.economy.researchSpending
      / 100;

    if (
      project.progress >=
      project.requiredProgress
    ) {

      const currentLevel =
        country.technology.domains[
          project.domain
        ];

      // If domain level is undefined, treat as 0 before incrementing
      country.technology.domains[
        project.domain
      ] = (currentLevel ?? 0) + 1;

      project.completed = true;
    }
  }

  country.technology.projects =
    country.technology.projects
      .filter(
        p => !p.completed
      );
}

}

========== D:\Pax Historia LOCAL\server\src\routes\game.ts ==========

import express from "express";
import { createGame } from "../game/CreateGame";
import { runTurn } from "../game/RunTurn";
import { TimeStep } from "../time/TimeStep";
import { ScenarioRegistry } from "../scenarios/ScenarioRegistry";

const router = express.Router();

// РҐСЂР°РЅРёР»РёС‰Рµ РёРіСЂС‹ (РІ РїСЂРѕРґР°РєС€РµРЅРµ РёСЃРїРѕР»СЊР·РѕРІР°С‚СЊ Р‘Р”)
let currentGame: any = null;

router.post("/start", (req, res) => {
  const { scenarioId, playerCountryId } = req.body;
  
  if (!ScenarioRegistry[scenarioId as keyof typeof ScenarioRegistry]) {
    res.status(400).json({ error: "Invalid scenario" });
    return;
  }
  
  currentGame = createGame(
    scenarioId as keyof typeof ScenarioRegistry, 
    playerCountryId
  );
  res.json(currentGame);
});

router.get("/state", (req, res) => {
  if (!currentGame) {
    res.status(404).json({ error: "No active game" });
    return;
  }
  res.json(currentGame);
});

router.post("/next-turn", (req, res) => {
  if (!currentGame) {
    res.status(404).json({ error: "No active game" });
    return;
  }
  
  runTurn(currentGame, TimeStep.OneMonth);
  res.json(currentGame);
});

export default router;

========== D:\Pax Historia LOCAL\server\src\simulation\economy\EconomyTick.ts ==========

import { type Country } from "@shared/types/Country";
import { ResourceType } from "@shared/types/resources/ResourcesType";
import { RESOURCE_WEIGHTS as resourceWeights } from "@shared/constants/resourceWeights";

export function economyTick(
  country: Country
): void {

  const economy = country.economy;

  const income =
    economy.taxRevenue +
    economy.exportIncome +
    economy.stateEnterpriseIncome +
    economy.otherIncome;

  const expenses =
    economy.militarySpending +
    economy.researchSpending +
    economy.educationSpending +
    economy.infrastructureSpending +
    economy.welfareSpending +
    economy.debtInterest +
    economy.otherExpenses;

  economy.budgetBalance =
    income - expenses;

  economy.treasury +=
    economy.budgetBalance;

  const growthRate = 0.002;

  economy.gdp *=
    1 + growthRate;

  economy.inflation +=
    0.1 * (expenses - income)
    / economy.gdp;

  economy.unemployment +=
    0.05 * (expenses - income)
    / economy.gdp;

  economy.unemployment =
    Math.max(
      0,
      economy.unemployment
    );

  let resourceBonus = 0;

  for (const resource of Object.values(ResourceType)) {

    const amount =
      country.stockpile[resource];

    const weight =
      resourceWeights[resource] ?? 0;

    resourceBonus += amount * weight;
  }
}

========== D:\Pax Historia LOCAL\server\src\simulation\military\MilitaryTick.ts ==========

import { type Country } from "@shared/types/Country";

export function militaryTick(
  country: Country
): void {

  for (
    const unit of
    country.military.units
  ) {

    if (
      unit.strength < 100
    ) {

      unit.strength += 1;
    }
  }
}

}

========== D:\Pax Historia LOCAL\server\src\simulation\research\canResearch.ts ==========

import { type Country } from "@shared/types/Country";
import { type TechnologyDefinition } from "@shared/types/research/TechnologyDefinition";

export function canResearch(
    country: Country,
    technology: TechnologyDefinition
): boolean {

    for (
        const prerequisite
        of technology.prerequisites
    ) {

        if (
            !country.researchedTechnologyIds
                .includes(prerequisite)
        ) {

            return false;
        }
    }

    return true;
}

========== D:\Pax Historia LOCAL\server\src\simulation\research\ResearchTick.ts ==========

import { type Country } from "@shared/types/Country";
import { type ResearchProject } from "@shared/types/research/ResearchProject";
import { ResourceType } from "@shared/types/resources/ResourcesType";

export function researchTick(
  country: Country
): void {

  for (
    const project of
    country.technology.projects
  ) {

    const techSatisfied =
      project.requiredTechnologyIds.every(
        id =>
          country.researchedTechnologyIds.includes(id)
      );

    const resourcesSatisfied =
      Object.entries(
        project.requiredResources
      ).every(
        ([resourceType, amount]) =>
          country.stockpile[
          resourceType as ResourceType
          ] >= amount
      );

    if (
      !techSatisfied ||
      !resourcesSatisfied
    ) {
      continue;
    }

    project.progress +=
      project.progressPerMonth *
      (
        country.economy.researchSpending
        / project.cost
      );

    if (
      project.progress >=
      project.requiredProgress
    ) {

      project.completed = true;

      const currentLevel =
        country.technology.domains[
        project.domain
        ] ?? 0;

      country.technology.domains[
        project.domain
      ] = currentLevel + 1;
    }
  }

  country.technology.projects =
    country.technology.projects.filter(
      p => !p.completed
    );
}

========== D:\Pax Historia LOCAL\server\src\simulation\resources\ResourceTick.ts ==========

import { type Country } from "@shared/types/Country";
import { type Region } from "@shared/types/map/Region";

export function resourceTick(
  country: Country,
  regions: Region[]
): void {

  const ownedRegions =
    regions.filter(
      region =>
        region.ownerCountryId ===
        country.id
    );

  for (
    const region of ownedRegions
  ) {

    for (const [resource, amount] of Object.entries(region.resourceProduction)) {
      const key = resource as keyof typeof country.stockpile;
      country.stockpile[key] += amount;
    }
  }
}

========== D:\Pax Historia LOCAL\server\src\simulation\SimulationEngine.ts ==========

import { type GameState } from "@shared/types/GameState";
import { resourceTick } from "./resources/ResourceTick";
import { researchTick } from "./research/ResearchTick";
import { economyTick } from "./economy/EconomyTick";
import { populationTick } from "./population/PopulationTick";
import { militaryTick } from "./military/MilitaryTick";

export function simulateMonth(
    game: GameState
): void {
    for (const country of game.countries) {

        economyTick(country);

        resourceTick(country, game.regions);

        researchTick(country);

        populationTick(country);

        militaryTick(country);
    }
}

========== D:\Pax Historia LOCAL\server\src\time\AdvanceTime.ts ==========

import { type GameState } from "@shared/types/GameState";
import { TimeStep } from "./TimeStep";

export function advanceTime(
  game: GameState,
  step: TimeStep
): void {

  const date =
    new Date(game.currentDate);

  date.setMonth(
    date.getMonth() + step
  );

  game.currentDate =
    date.toISOString().slice(0, 10);
}

  OneMonth = 1,

========== D:\Pax Historia LOCAL\server\src\index.ts ==========

import express from "express";
import cors from "cors";
import gameRoutes from "./routes/game";
import playerRoutes from "./routes/player";
import scenarioRoutes from "./routes/scenarios";

const app = express();
app.use(cors());
app.use(express.json());
app.use("/game", gameRoutes);
app.use("/player", playerRoutes);
app.use("/scenarios", scenarioRoutes);

app.listen(3000, () => {
  console.log("Server started");
});

========== D:\Pax Historia LOCAL\shared\src\constants\createEmptyStockpile.ts ==========

import { ResourceType } from "../types/resources/ResourcesType";
import { ResourceStockpile } from "../types/resources/ResourceStockpile";

export function createEmptyStockpile(): ResourceStockpile {
  return Object.values(ResourceType).reduce((stockpile, type) =>  {
    if (typeof type === "string") {
      stockpile[type as ResourceType] = 0;
    }
    return stockpile;
  }, {} as ResourceStockpile);
}

========== D:\Pax Historia LOCAL\shared\src\utils\createTechnologyState.ts ==========

import { TechnologyState } from "../types/TechnologyState";

export function createTechnologyState(
  domains: string[]
): TechnologyState {

  const technologyDomains:
    Record<string, number> = {};

  for (const domain of domains) {

    technologyDomains[domain] = 0;
  }

  return {

    domains: technologyDomains,

    projects: []
  };
}

========== D:\Pax Historia LOCAL\shared\src\utils\getEraByYear.ts ==========

import { ERAS } from "../data/eras";


export function getEraByYear(
  year: number
) {

  return ERAS.find(
    era =>
      year >= era.startYear &&
      year <= era.endYear
  );
}
